# <a name="required-diagnostic-data-for-office"></a><span data-ttu-id="52983-103">Nepieciešamie Office diagnostikas dati</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-103">Required diagnostic data for Office</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="52983-104">Informācija šajā rakstā attiecas uz tālāk minētās Office klienta programmatūras versiju 1904 vai jaunāku versiju, kas instalēta datorā, kurā darbojas sistēma Windows:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-104">The information in this article applies to Version 1904 or later of the following Office client software installed on a computer running Windows:</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="52983-105">Office 365 ProPlus un Office 365 Business</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-105">Office 365 ProPlus and Office 365 Business</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="52983-106">Office 365 individuālai lietošanai, Office 365 mājas lietošanai vai citas Office versijas, kas ir daļa no Office 365 abonementa.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-106">Office 365 Personal, Office 365 Home, or other versions of Office that are part of an Office 365 subscription.</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="52983-107">Project un Visio, kas ir iekļautas dažos abonēšanas plānos, piemēram, Project Online Professional plānā vai Visio Online 2. plānā.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-107">Project and Visio that come with some subscription plans, such as the Project Online Professional plan or Visio Online Plan 2.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52983-108">Diagnostikas dati tiek izmantoti, lai uzturētu Office drošu un atjauninātu, noteiktu, diagnosticētu un novērstu problēmas, kā arī uzlabotu produktu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-108">Diagnostic data is used to keep Office secure and up-to-date, detect, diagnose and fix problems, and also make product improvements.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-109">Šie dati neietver lietotāja vārdu vai e-pasta adresi, failu saturu vai informāciju par programmām, kas nav saistītas ar Office.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-109">This data does not include a user’s name or email address, the content of the user’s files, or information about apps unrelated to Office.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52983-110">Šie diagnostikas dati tiek apkopoti un nosūtīti korporācijai Microsoft par Office klienta programmatūru, kas tiek lietota datoros, kuros darbojas operētājsistēma Windows.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-110">This diagnostic data is collected and sent to Microsoft about Office client software being used on computers running Windows.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-111">Daži diagnostikas dati ir nepieciešami, bet daži diagnostikas dati ir neobligāti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-111">Some diagnostic data is required, while some diagnostic data is optional.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-112">Piedāvājam jums iespēju izvēlēties, vai sūtīt mums nepieciešamos vai neobligātos diagnostikas datus, izmantojot tādus konfidencialitātes kontroles līdzekļus kā organizācijas politikas iestatījumus.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-112">We give you the ability to choose whether to send us required or optional diagnostic data through the use of privacy controls, such as policy settings for organizations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-113">Mums sūtāmos diagnostikas datus varat skatīt, izmantojot diagnostikas datu skatītāju.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-113">You can see the diagnostic data being sent to us by using the Diagnostic Data Viewer.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52983-114">***Nepieciešamie diagnostikas dati*** ir minimālie dati, kas nepieciešami, lai Office uzturētu drošu, atjauninātu un ar paredzēto veiktspēju atbilstošajā ierīcē.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-114">***Required diagnostic data*** is the minimum data necessary to help keep Office secure, up-to-date, and performing as expected on the device it’s installed on.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52983-115">Nepieciešamie diagnostikas dati palīdz noteikt ar Office saistītas problēmas, kuru cēlonis var būt saistīts ar ierīces vai programmatūras konfigurāciju.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-115">Required diagnostic data helps to identify problems with Office that may be related to a device or software configuration.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-116">Piemēram, tie var palīdzēt noteikt, vai Office līdzeklis biežāk avarē noteiktā operētājsistēmas versijā, kopā ar nesen ieviestiem līdzekļiem vai tad, kad ir atspējoti konkrēti Office līdzekļi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-116">For example, it can help determine if an Office feature crashes more frequently on a particular operating system version, with newly introduced features, or when certain Office features are disabled.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-117">Nepieciešamie diagnostikas dati palīdz mums ātrāk noteikt, diagnosticēt un novērst problēmas, lai mazinātu ietekmi uz lietotājiem vai organizācijām.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-117">Required diagnostic data helps us detect, diagnose, and fix these problems more quickly so the impact to users or organizations is reduced.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52983-118">Papildinformāciju par diagnostikas datiem lasiet šajos rakstos:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-118">For more information about diagnostic data, see the following:</span></span>

- [<span data-ttu-id="52983-119">Neobligātie Office diagnostikas dati</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-119">Optional diagnostic data for Office</span></span>](optional-diagnostic-data.md)
- [<span data-ttu-id="52983-120">Diagnostikas datu skatītāja izmantošana ar Office</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-120">Using the Diagnostic Data Viewer with Office</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/cf761ce9-d805-4c60-a339-4e07f3182855)

<span data-ttu-id="52983-121">Ja esat organizācijas administrators, iespējams, jūs interesēs arī šie raksti:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-121">If you’re the admin for your organization, you might also be interested in the following:</span></span>

- [<span data-ttu-id="52983-122">Pārskats par konfidencialitātes kontroles līdzekļiem pakalpojumā Office 365 ProPlus</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-122">Overview of privacy controls for Office 365 ProPlus</span></span>](overview-privacy-controls.md)
- [<span data-ttu-id="52983-123">Politikas iestatījumu izmantošana Office 365 ProPlus konfidencialitātes kontroles pārvaldībai</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-123">Use policy settings to manage privacy controls for Office 365 ProPlus</span></span>](manage-privacy-controls.md)

## <a name="categories-data-subtypes-events-and-data-fields-for-required-diagnostic-data"></a><span data-ttu-id="52983-124">Nepieciešamo diagnostikas datu kategorijas, datu apakštipi, notikumi un datu lauki</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-124">Categories, data subtypes, events, and data fields for required diagnostic data</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52983-125">Nepieciešamie diagnostikas dati tiek organizēti kategorijās un datu apakštipos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-125">Required diagnostic data is organized into categories and data subtypes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-126">Katrā datu apakštipā ir notikumi, kuros ir datu lauki, kas attiecas uz konkrēto notikumu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-126">Within each data subtype are events, which contain data fields that are specific to that event.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52983-127">Tālāk tabulā ir sniegts saraksts, kurā ir norādītas nepieciešamo diagnostikas datu kategorijas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-127">The following table provides a list of the categories for required diagnostic data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-128">Ir uzskaitīti katras kategorijas datu apakštipi un datu apakštipa svarīgāko aspektu apraksts.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-128">The data subtypes within each category are listed, along with a description of the focus for that data subtype.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-129">Norādītas arī saites uz katru datu apakštipa sadaļu, kurā var atrast tālāk norādīto informāciju.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-129">There are links to each data subtype section where you’ll find the following information:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="52983-130">Notikumu saraksts konkrētajā datu apakštipā</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-130">A list of events in that data subtype</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="52983-131">Katra notikuma apraksts</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-131">A description of each event</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="52983-132">Datu lauku saraksts katrā notikumā</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-132">A list of data fields in each event</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="52983-133">Katra datu lauka apraksts</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-133">A description of each data field</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="52983-134">**Kategorija**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-134">**Category**</span></span>       | <span data-ttu-id="52983-135">**Datu apakštips**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-135">**Data subtype**</span></span>| <span data-ttu-id="52983-136">**Apraksts**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-136">**Description**</span></span>    |
| ---------- | ------------- | ---- |
| <span data-ttu-id="52983-137">**Programmatūras iestatīšana un inventārs**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-137">**Software setup and inventory**</span></span> | [<span data-ttu-id="52983-138">Office iestatīšana un inventārs</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-138">Office setup and inventory</span></span>](#office-setup-and-inventory-subtype)   | <span data-ttu-id="52983-139">Instalētais produkts, versija un instalēšanas statuss.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-139">Installed product and version and the installation status.</span></span>  |
| | [<span data-ttu-id="52983-140">Office pievienojumprogrammu konfigurācija</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-140">Office add-in configuration</span></span>](#office-add-in-configuration-subtype)  | <span data-ttu-id="52983-141">Programmatūras pievienojumprogrammas un to iestatījumi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-141">Software add-ins and their settings.</span></span>     |
| | [<span data-ttu-id="52983-142">Drošība</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-142">Security</span></span>](#security-subtype)  | <span data-ttu-id="52983-143">Dokumenta, līdzekļa un pievienojumprogrammas kļūdas nosacījumi, kas var negatīvi ietekmēt drošību, tostarp produktu atjauninājumu gatavību.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-143">Document, feature, and add-in error conditions that may compromise security, including product update readiness.</span></span>  |
| <span data-ttu-id="52983-144">**Produktu un pakalpojumu lietojums**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-144">**Product and service usage**</span></span>    | [<span data-ttu-id="52983-145">Lietojumprogrammas līdzekļu sekmju novērtējums</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-145">Application feature success</span></span>](#application-feature-success-subtype)   | <span data-ttu-id="52983-146">Informācija par sekmīgu lietojumprogrammas funkcionalitāti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-146">Success of application functionality.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-147">Attiecas tikai uz programmas un dokumentu atvēršanu un aizvēršanu, failu rediģēšana un failu koplietošanu (sadarbību).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-147">Limited to opening and closing of the application and documents, file editing, and file sharing (collaboration).</span></span> |
| | [<span data-ttu-id="52983-148">Lietojumprogrammas statuss un palaišana</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-148">Application status and boot</span></span>](#application-status-and-boot-subtype)    | <span data-ttu-id="52983-149">Nosaka, vai ir notikuši konkrēti līdzekļu notikumi, piemēram, startēšana vai apturēšana, un vai līdzeklis darbojas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-149">Determination if specific feature events have occurred, such as start or stop, and if feature is running.</span></span>   |
| | [<span data-ttu-id="52983-150">Office pieejamības konfigurācija</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-150">Office accessibility configuration</span></span>](#office-accessibility-configuration-subtype)  | <span data-ttu-id="52983-151">Office pieejamības līdzekļi</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-151">Office accessibility features</span></span>       |
| <span data-ttu-id="52983-152">**Produktu un pakalpojumu veiktspēja**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-152">**Product and service performance**</span></span>       | [<span data-ttu-id="52983-153">Neparedzēts lietojumprogrammas darbības pārtraukums (avārijas)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-153">Unexpected application exit (crash)</span></span>](#unexpected-application-exit-crash-subtype)  | <span data-ttu-id="52983-154">Neparedzēts lietojumprogrammas darbības pārtraukums un programmas statuss brīdī, kad tas notika.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-154">Unexpected application exits and the state of the application when that happens.</span></span>    |
|  | [<span data-ttu-id="52983-155">Lietojumprogrammas līdzekļu novērtējums</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-155">Application feature performance </span></span>](#application-feature-performance-subtype)  | <span data-ttu-id="52983-156">Slikts atbildes laiks vai slikta veiktspēja tādos scenārijos kā programmas startēšana vai faila atvēršana.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-156">Poor response time or performance for scenarios such as application start up or opening a file.</span></span> |
|  | [<span data-ttu-id="52983-157">Lietojumprogrammas darbības kļūda</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-157">Application activity error</span></span>](#application-activity-error-subtype)   | <span data-ttu-id="52983-158">Līdzekļa funkcionalitātes vai lietošanas iespēju kļūdas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-158">Errors in functionality of a feature or user experience.</span></span>  |
| <span data-ttu-id="52983-159">**Ierīču savienojamība un konfigurācija**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-159">**Device connectivity and configuration**</span></span> | [<span data-ttu-id="52983-160">Ierīču savienojamība un konfigurācija</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-160">Device connectivity and configuration</span></span>](#device-connectivity-and-configuration-subtype) | <span data-ttu-id="52983-161">Tīkla savienojuma statuss un ierīces iestatījumi, piemēram, atmiņas iestatījumi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-161">Network connection state and device settings, such as memory.</span></span> |


> [!NOTE]
> - <span data-ttu-id="52983-162">Kategorijas tiek rādītas datu diagnostikas skatītājā, bet datu apakštipi netiek rādīti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-162">Categories are shown in the Diagnostic Data Viewer, but data subtypes are not shown.</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="52983-163">Datu lauks, kas atzīmēts kā *novecojis*, ir noņemts vai drīz tiks noņemts no nepieciešamajiem diagnostikas datiem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-163">A data field marked *Obsolete* has been or will soon be removed from required diagnostic data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-164">Daži no šiem datu laukiem ir dublikāti, kas tika izveidoti diagnostikas datu modernizēšanas rezultātā un kas tika izmantoti, lai nodrošinātu nepārtrauktu pakalpojuma darbību reāllaika diagnostikas pārraudzības atskaitēm.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-164">Some of these data fields are duplicates that arose as diagnostic data was modernized and were used to ensure no service disruption to live diagnostic monitoring reports.</span></span>

## <a name="categories-and-data-fields-that-are-common-for-all-events"></a><span data-ttu-id="52983-165">Kategorijas un datu lauki, kas ir kopīgi visiem notikumiem</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-165">Categories and data fields that are common for all events</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52983-166">Neatkarīgi no kategorijas vai datu apakštipa pastāv informācija par notikumiem, kas attiecas uz visiem notikumiem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-166">There is some information about events that is common to all events, regardless of category or data subtype.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-167">Šī kopīgā informācija, ko dažkārt dēvē par *datu līgumiem*, ir sakārtota kategorijās.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-167">This common information, which is sometimes referred to as *data contracts*, is organized into categories.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-168">Katrā kategorijā ir lauki, un šie lauki ir atsevišķa notikuma metadati un rekvizīti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-168">Each category contains fields, and these fields are the metadata and properties of an individual event.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-169">Šo informāciju varat skatīt, izmantojot diagnostikas datu skatītāju.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-169">You can view this information by using the Diagnostic Data Viewer.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52983-170">Kategorijas, kurās ir apkopota informācija par notikumiem, var iedalīt divās grupās:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-170">The categories of information that is collected about events can be divided into two groups:</span></span>

  - [<span data-ttu-id="52983-171">Informācija, kas ir kopīga visiem notikumiem</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-171">Information common to all events</span></span>](#information-common-to-all-events)
  - [<span data-ttu-id="52983-172">Informācija, kas īpaši atbalsta diagnostikas datu apkopošanu</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-172">Information that specifically supports diagnostic data collection</span></span>](#information-that-specifically-supports-diagnostic-data-collection)

### <a name="information-common-to-all-events"></a><span data-ttu-id="52983-173">*Informācija, kas ir kopīga visiem notikumiem*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-173">*Information common to all events*</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52983-174">Informācija, kas ir kopīga visiem notikumiem, tiek apkopota tālāk norādītajās kategorijās.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-174">Information common to all events is collected in the following categories.</span></span>

#### <a name="app"></a><span data-ttu-id="52983-175">Programma</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-175">App</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="52983-176">Informācija par lietojumprogrammu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-176">Information about the application.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-177">Visi lauki ir konstanti visām attiecīgās lietojumprogrammas versijas sesijām.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-177">All fields are constant for all sessions of a given application version.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52983-178">Šajā kategorijā ir šādi lauki:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-178">This category contains the following fields:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-179">**Branch** — zars, no kura nāk attiecīgā būvējuma versija.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-179">**Branch** - The branch that the given build came from.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-180">Ļauj mums noteikt, no kāda zara tipa nāk attiecīgais būvējums, lai mēs varētu pareizi piemērot labojumus.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-180">Allows us to determine what type of branch a given build came from so that we can correctly target fixes.</span></span>
  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-181">**InstallType** — skaitītājs, kas norāda, kā lietotājs ir instalējis lietojumprogrammu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-181">**InstallType** - An enumerator that identifies how the user installed the application.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-182">Ļauj mums noteikt, vai konkrēti instalēšanas mehānismi rada problēmas, kas nav sastopamas citos instalēšanas mehānismos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-182">Allows us to determine if specific install mechanisms are creating issues that are not seen in other installation mechanisms.</span></span>
  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-183">**Name** — tās lietojumprogrammas nosaukums, kas nodrošina datus.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-183">**Name** - The name of the application that is providing the data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-184">Ļauj mums noteikt, kuras lietojumprogrammas darbībā ir radušās problēmas, lai mēs tās varētu atrisināt.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-184">Allows us to identify which application is showing an issue so we know how to address it.</span></span>
  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-185">**Platform** — tās platformas plašā klasifikācija, kurā darbojas programma.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-185">**Platform** - The broad classification of the platform on which the app is running.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-186">Ļauj mums noteikt platformas, kurās, iespējams, ir radusies problēma, lai mēs varētu pareizi noteikt problēmas prioritāti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-186">Allows us to identify on which platforms an issue may be occurring so that we can correctly prioritize the issue.</span></span>
  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-187">**Version** — lietojumprogrammas versija.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-187">**Version** - The version of the application.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-188">Ļauj mums noteikt, kurās produkta versijās ir radusies problēma, lai mēs varētu pareizi noteikt tās prioritāti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-188">Allows us to identify which versions of the product are showing an issue so that we can correctly prioritize it.</span></span>

#### <a name="client"></a><span data-ttu-id="52983-189">Klients</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-189">Client</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="52983-190">Identifikators, kas ir saistīts ar Office instanci ierīcē.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-190">Identifier related to an Office instance on a device.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-191">Konstants visām attiecīgās vairāku programmu komplektu instalācijas versijas programmu sesijām vai arī visām attiecīgās lietojumprogrammas versijas sesijām.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-191">Constant for all sessions of all apps of a given installation version for multi-app suites, or constant for all sessions of a given application version.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52983-192">Šajā kategorijā ir šādi lauki:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-192">This category contains the following fields:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-193">**Id** — unikāls identifikators, kas ir piešķirts klientam Office instalēšanas laikā.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-193">**Id** - Unique identifier assigned to a client at install time of Office.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-194">Ļauj mums noteikt, vai problēmas ietekmē atlasītu instalāciju kopu, un ietekmēto lietotāju skaitu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-194">Allows us to identify whether issues are impacting a select set of installs and how many users are impacted.</span></span>

#### <a name="consent"></a><span data-ttu-id="52983-195">Atļauja</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-195">Consent</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52983-196">Informācija saistībā ar lietotāja piekrišanu diagnostikas datiem un saistītajiem līdzekļiem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-196">Information regarding the users consent for diagnostic data and connected experiences.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52983-197">Šajā kategorijā ir šādi lauki:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-197">This category contains the following fields:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-198">**UserCategory** — norāda tā lietotāja tipu, kas sniedza atļauju.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-198">**UserCategory –** Identified the type of user who made the consent.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-199">Kāds no MSAUser, AADUser vai LocalDeviceUser</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-199">One of MSAUser, AADUser or LocalDeviceUser</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-200">**DiagnosticConsentLevel** — norāda, kāds diagnostikas datu atļaujas līmenis ir piešķirts lietotājam</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-200">**DiagnosticConsentLevel** – Indicates what level of diagnostic data consent the user has given</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-201">**DiagnosticConsentSourceLocation** — norāda, kā lietotājs ir iesniedzis atļauju diagnostikas datiem</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-201">**DiagnosticConsentSourceLocation** – Indicates how the user had provided the consent for diagnostic data</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-202">**DiagnosticConsentConsentTime** — norāda, kad lietotājs ir iesniedzis atļauju diagnostikas datiem</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-202">**DiagnosticConsentConsentTime** – Indicates when the user provided the consent for diagnostic data</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-203">**ServiceConnectionState** — norāda, vai lietotājs ir izvēlējies lietot vai nelietot visus saistītos līdzekļus</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-203">**ServiceConnectionState** – Indicates whether the user has chosen to use or not use all connected experiences</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-204">**ServiceConnectionStateSourceLocation** — norāda, kā lietotājs ir izvēlējies lietot vai nelietot visus saistītos līdzekļus</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-204">**ServiceConnectionStateSourceLocation** – Indicates how the user provided the choice whether to use all connected experiences</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-205">**ServiceConnectionStateConsentTime** — norāda, kad lietotājs ir izvēlējies lietot vai nelietot visus saistītos līdzekļus</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-205">**ServiceConnectionStateConsentTime** – Indicates when the user chose whether to use all connected experiences</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-206">**ControllerConnectedServicesState** — norāda, vai lietotājam ir piekļuve neobligātajiem saistītajiem līdzekļiem</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-206">**ControllerConnectedServicesState** – Indicates whether the user has access to optional connected experiences</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-207">**ControllerConnectedServicesStateSourceLocation** — norāda, kā tika veikta lietotāja izvēle lietot neobligātos saistītos līdzekļus</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-207">**ControllerConnectedServicesStateSourceLocation** – Indicates how the user’s choice for optional connected experiences was made</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-208">**ControllerConnectedServicesStateConsentTime** — norāda, kad lietotājs izvēlējās neobligāto saistīto līdzekļu statusu</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-208">**ControllerConnectedServicesStateConsentTime** – Indicates when the user chose the status of optional connected experiences</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-209">**UserContentDependentState** — norāda, vai lietotājs ir izvēlējies iespējot vai atspējot saistītos līdzekļus, kas analizē saturu</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-209">**UserContentDependentState** – Indicates whether the user has chosen to enable or disable connected experiences that analyze content</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-210">**UserContentDependentStateSourceLocation** — norāda, kā tika veikta lietotāja izvēle iespējot vai atspējot saistītos līdzekļus, kas analizē saturu</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-210">**UserContentDependentStateSourceLocation** – Indicates how the user’s choice to enable or disable was made for connected experiences that analyze content</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-211">**UserContentDependentStateConsentTime** — norāda, kad lietotājs izvēlējās iespējot vai atspējot saistītos līdzekļus, kas analizē saturu</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-211">**UserContentDependentStateConsentTime** – Indicates when the user chose to enable or disable connected experiences that analyze content was made</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-212">**DownloadContentState** — norāda, vai lietotājs ir izvēlējies iespējot vai atspējot saistītos līdzekļus, kas lejupielādē tiešsaistes saturu</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-212">**DownloadContentState** – Indicates whether the user has chosen to enable or disable connected experiences that download online content</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-213">**DownloadContentStateSourceLocation** — norāda, kā lietotājs izvēlējās iespējot vai atspējot saistītos līdzekļus, kas lejupielādē tiešsaistes saturu</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-213">**DownloadContentStateSourceLocation** – Indicates how the user made the choice to enable or disable connected experiences that that download online content</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-214">**DownloadContentStateConsentTime** — norāda, kad lietotājs izvēlējās iespējot vai atspējot saistītos līdzekļus, kas lejupielādē tiešsaistes saturu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-214">**DownloadContentStateConsentTime** – Indicates when the user made the choice to enable or disable connected experiences that download online content.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52983-223">Nodrošina programmas ID un operētājsistēmas versiju saderībai ar esošajām mantotās kolekcijas darbībām.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-223">Provides an App Id and OS version for compatibility with existing legacy collection practices.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-227">**OsEnv** — skaitītājs, kas norāda operētājsistēmu, kurā darbojas sesija.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-227">**OsEnv** - An enumerator indicating which operating system the session is running on.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-228">Ļauj mums noteikt, kurā operētājsistēmā ir radusies problēma, lai mēs varētu noteikt problēmu prioritāti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-228">Allows us to identify which operating system an issue happening on so we can prioritize issues.</span></span>

#### <a name="release"></a><span data-ttu-id="52983-229">Laidiens</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-229">Release</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="52983-230">Informācija saistībā ar laidiena kanālu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-230">Information related to the release channel.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-231">Visi lauki ir konstanti visām attiecīgās instalācijas versijas programmu sesijām.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-231">All fields are constant for all sessions of all apps of a given installation version.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-232">Norāda to ierīču grupu, kas atrodas vienā produkta laidiena cikla posmā.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-232">Identifies a group of devices all in one phase of a product release cycle.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52983-233">Šajā kategorijā ir šādi lauki:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-233">This category contains the following fields:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-234">**Audience** — norāda konkrētās auditorijas grupas apakšauditoriju.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-234">**Audience** - Identifies a sub-audience of a given audience group.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-235">Ļauj mums izsekot auditorijas grupu apakškopām, lai novērtētu problēmu izplatību un noteiktu to prioritāti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-235">Allows us to track subsets of audience groups to evaluate prevalence and prioritization of issues.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-236">**AudienceGroup** — norāda loku, no kura nāk dati.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-236">**AudienceGroup** - Identifies the ring where data is coming from.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-237">Ļauj mums pakāpeniski izlaist līdzekļus un identificēt potenciālās problēmas, pirms lielākā daļa lietotāju ir ar tām saskārušās.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-237">Allows us to roll out features in a staged fashion and identify potential issues before they reach most users.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-238">**Channel** — kanāls, kurā tiek izlaists produkts.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-238">**Channel** - The channel that the product is being released through.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-239">Ļauj mums noteikt, vai problēma ietekmē kādu no mūsu izlaišanas kanāliem citādi nekā citus.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-239">Allows us to identify if an issue is impacting one of our rollout channels differently than others.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-240">**Fork** — norāda produkta sazarojumu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-240">**Fork** - Identifies the fork of the product.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-241">Ļauj izmantot mehānismu, lai apkopotu būvējumu numuru kopu datus nolūkā identificēt problēmas saistībā ar konkrēto laidienu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-241">Allows a mechanism to aggregate data across a set of build numbers to identify issues related to a given release.</span></span>

#### <a name="session"></a><span data-ttu-id="52983-242">Sesija</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-242">Session</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="52983-243">Informācija par procesa sesiju.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-243">Information about the process session.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-244">Visi šīs sesijas lauki ir konstanti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-244">All fields are constant for this session.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52983-245">Šajā kategorijā ir šādi lauki:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-245">This category contains the following fields:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-246">**ABConfigs** — norāda testējamo variantu kopu, kas darbojas konkrētajā sesijā.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-246">**ABConfigs** - Identifies the set of flights that are running in a given session.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-247">Ļauj mums noteikt, kuri konkrētie testējamie varianti darbojas sesijā, lai mēs varētu noteikt, vai testējamā versija ir tās problēmas cēlonis, kas ietekmē lietotājus.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-247">Allows us to identify which individual flights are running on a session so that we can determine if a flight is the source of an issue impacting users.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-248">**EcsETag** — indikators no testējamo variantu sistēmas, kas apzīmē mašīnai nosūtītos testējamos variantus.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-248">**EcsETag** - An indicator from the flighting system that represents the flights sent to the machine.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-249">Ļauj mums noteikt, kuri testējamie varianti, iespējams, ietekmē attiecīgo sesiju.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-249">Allows us to identify what flights might be impacting a given session.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-250">**Flags** — karodziņi, kas izseko bitmasku un attiecas uz visu sesiju. Pašlaik galvenā uzmanība tiek pievērsta iztveršanai un diagnostikas datu opcijām.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-250">**Flags** - Bitmask tracking flags applicable to an entire session, currently primarily focused on sampling and diagnostic data options.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-251">Ļauj mums kontrolēt attiecīgās sesijas darbību saistībā ar sesijas ģenerētajiem diagnostikas datiem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-251">Allows us to control how a given session behaves in relation to the diagnostic data that the session generates.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-252">**Id** — unikāli identificē attiecīgo datu sesiju.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-252">**Id** - Uniquely identifies a given session of data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-253">Ļauj mums noteikt problēmu ietekmi, izvērtējot ietekmēto sesiju skaitu un nosakot, vai šīm sesijām ir kopīgi līdzekļi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-253">Allows us to identify the impact of issues by evaluating the number of sessions that are impacted and if there are common features of those sessions.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-254">**ImpressionId** — norāda testējamo variantu kopu, kas darbojas konkrētajā sesijā.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-254">**ImpressionId** - Identifies the set of flights that are running in a given session.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-255">Ļauj mums noteikt, kuri konkrētie testējamie varianti darbojas sesijā, lai mēs varētu noteikt, vai testējamā versija ir tās problēmas cēlonis, kas ietekmē lietotājus.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-255">Allows us to identify which individual flights are running on a session so that we can determine if a flight is the source of an issue impacting users.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-256">**MeasuresEnabled** — karodziņš, kas norāda, vai pašreizējie sesijas dati tiek iztverti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-256">**MeasuresEnabled** - Flag indicating if the current sessions data is sampled or not.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-257">Ļauj mums noteikt, kā statistiski izvērtēt datus, kas tiek apkopoti no attiecīgās sesijas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-257">Allows us to determine how to statistically evaluate the data that is gathered from the given session.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-258">**SamplingClientId** — klienta ID, kas tiek izmantots, lai noteiktu, vai tas ir daļa no iztveršanas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-258">**SamplingClientId** - The id of the client used to determine if it is part of sampling.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-259">Ļauj mums noteikt, kāpēc konkrēta sesija tika iekļauta vai neiekļauta iztveršanā.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-259">Allows us to determine why an individual session was included or excluded from sampling.</span></span>

#### <a name="user"></a><span data-ttu-id="52983-260">Lietotājs</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-260">User</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52983-261">Sniedz komerciālās programmatūras SKU informāciju par nomnieku.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-261">Provides tenant information for commercial software SKUs.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52983-262">Šajā kategorijā ir šādi lauki:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-262">This category contains the following fields:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-263">**PrimaryIdentityHash** — identifikatora pseidonīms, kas apzīmē pašreizējo lietotāju.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-263">**PrimaryIdentityHash** – A pseudonymous identifier that represents the current user.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-264">**PrimaryIdentitySpace** — tās identitātes tips, kas atrodas šeit: PrimaryIdentityHash.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-264">**PrimaryIdentitySpace** – The type of identity contained in the PrimaryIdentityHash.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-265">Kāds no MASCID, OrgIdCID vai UserObjectId.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-265">One of MASCID, OrgIdCID or UserObjectId.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-266">**TenantGroup** — tā nomnieka tips, kam pieder abonements.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-266">**TenantGroup** - The type of the tenant that the subscription belongs to.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-267">Ļauj mums klasificēt problēmas un noteikt, vai problēma ir plaši izplatīta vai izolēta lietotāju kopā.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-267">Allows us to classify issues and identify whether a problem is widespread or isolated to a set of users.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-268">**TenantId** — nomnieks, ar kuru ir saistīts lietotāja abonements.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-268">**TenantId** - The tenant that a user’s subscription is tied to.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-269">Ļauj mums klasificēt problēmas un noteikt, vai problēma ir plaši izplatīta vai izolēta konkrēta nomnieka lietotāju kopā.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-269">Allows us to classify issues and identify whether a problem is widespread or isolated to a set of users or a specific tenant.</span></span>

### <a name="information-that-specifically-supports-diagnostic-data-collection"></a><span data-ttu-id="52983-270">*Informācija, kas īpaši atbalsta diagnostikas datu apkopošanu*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-270">*Information that specifically supports diagnostic data collection*</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52983-271">Informācija, kas īpaši atbalsta diagnostikas datu apkopošanu, tiek apkopota tālāk norādītajās kategorijās.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-271">Information that specifically supports diagnostic data collection is collected in the following categories.</span></span>

#### <a name="activity"></a><span data-ttu-id="52983-272">Darbība</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-272">Activity</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52983-273">Informācija, lai izprastu paša pasākuma apkopošanas panākumus.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-273">Information to understand the success of the collection event itself.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52983-274">Šajā kategorijā ir šādi lauki:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-274">This category contains the following fields:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-275">**AggMode** — nosaka, kā sistēmai jāapkopo darbības rezultāti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-275">**AggMode** - Tells the system how to aggregate activity results.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-276">Ļauj mums samazināt no lietotāja mašīnas augšupielādētās informācijas apjomu, apkopojot darbības rezultātus vienā notikumā, kas tiek periodiski nosūtīts.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-276">Allows us to reduce the amount of information uploaded from a user’s machine by aggregating activity results into a single event that gets sent periodically.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-277">**Count** — notikušās darbības reižu skaits, ja skaits ir no apkopotā notikuma.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-277">**Count** - The number of times the activity happened if the count is from an aggregated event.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-278">Ļauj mums noteikt, cik bieži darbība izdevās vai neizdevās, pamatojoties uz darbības apkopošanas režīmu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-278">Allows us to determine how often an activity succeeded or failed based on the aggregation mode of the activity.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-279">**CV** — vērtība, kas norāda relāciju starp darbībām un pakārtotajām darbībām.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-279">**CV** - A value that identifies the relationship between activities and sub-activities.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-280">Ļauj mums atjaunot relāciju starp ligzdotajām darbībām.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-280">Allows us to rebuild the relationship between nested activities.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-281">**Duration** — darbības izpildei nepieciešamais laiks.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-281">**Duration** - The length of time the activity took to execute.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-282">Ļauj mums noteikt veiktspējas problēmas, kas negatīvi ietekmē lietotāju pieredzi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-282">Allows us to identify performance issues that are negatively impacting the users experience.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-283">**Result**.**Code** — lietojumprogrammas definēts kods, lai identificētu noteiktus rezultātus.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-283">**Result**.**Code** - An application defined code to identify a given results.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-284">Ļauj mums noteikt specifiskāku informāciju par konkrēto kļūmi, piemēram, kļūmes kodu, ko var izmantot, lai klasificētu un novērstu problēmas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-284">Allows us to determine more specific details of a given failure such as a failure code that can be used to classify and fix issues.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-285">**Result.Tag** — vesela skaitļa tags, kas nosaka atrašanās vietu kodā, kurā tika ģenerēts rezultāts.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-285">**Result.Tag** - An integer tag that identifies the location in code where the result was generated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-286">Ļauj mums skaidri noteikt atrašanās vietu kodā, kurā tika ģenerēts rezultāts, kas iespējo kļūmju klasifikāciju.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-286">Allows us to distinctly identify the location in code where a result was generated which enables classification of failures.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-287">**Result**.**Type** — rezultāta koda tips.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-287">**Result**.**Type** - The type of the result code.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-288">Norāda nosūtītā rezultātu koda tipu, lai varētu pareizi interpretēt vērtību.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-288">Identifies what type of result code was sent so that the value can be correctly interpreted.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-289">**Success** — karodziņš, kas norāda, vai darbība izdevās vai neizdevās.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-289">**Success** - A flag indicating if the activity succeeded or failed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-290">Ļauj mums noteikt, vai lietotāja veiktās darbības produktā ir sekmīgas vai nesekmīgas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-290">Allows us to determine if actions the user takes in the product are succeeding or failing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-291">Ļauj mums noteikt problēmas, kas ietekmē lietotāju.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-291">This allows us to identify issues that are impacting the user.</span></span>

#### <a name="application"></a><span data-ttu-id="52983-292">Lietojumprogramma</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-292">Application</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="52983-293">Informācija par tās lietojumprogrammas instalēšanu, par kuru tiek apkopoti notikumi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-293">Information about the installation of the application from which the events are being gathered.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52983-294">Šajā kategorijā ir šādi lauki:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-294">This category contains the following fields:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-295">**Architecture** — lietojumprogrammas arhitektūra.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-295">**Architecture** - The architecture of the application.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-296">Ļauj mums klasificēt kļūdas, kas var būt specifiskas lietojumprogrammas arhitektūrai.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-296">Let’s us classify errors that might be specific to an architecture of the application.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-297">**Click2RunPackageVersion** — tās tehnoloģijas Click-To-Run pakotnes versijas numurs, kas tika izmantota, lai instalētu programmu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-297">**Click2RunPackageVersion** - The version number of the Click-To-Run package that installed the app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-298">Ļauj mums identificēt ar iestatīšanu saistītās problēmas, nosakot tās instalēšanas programmas versiju, kas tika izmantota, lai instalētu Office.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-298">Allows us to identify which version of the installer was used to install Office so we can identify setup related issues.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-299">**DistributionChannel** — kanāls, kurā ir izvietota programma.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-299">**DistributionChannel** - The channel where the app was deployed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-300">Ļauj mums sadalīt ienākošos datus, lai mēs varētu noteikt, vai problēmas ietekmē auditoriju.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-300">Allows us to partition incoming data so we can determine if issues are impacting audiences.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-301">**InstallMethod** — vai pašreizējais Office būvējums tika jaunināts, atritināts vai instalēts no jauna.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-301">**InstallMethod** - Whether the current build of Office was upgraded from an older build, rolled back to an older build, or a fresh install.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-302">**IsClickToRunInstall** — karodziņš, kas norāda, vai tika veikta Click-To-Run instalācija.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-302">**IsClickToRunInstall** - Flag indicating if install was a click to run install.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-303">Ļauj mums noteikt problēmas, kas varētu būt specifiskas Click-To-Run instalēšanas mehānismam.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-303">Allows us to identify issues that might be specific to the Click-To-Run install mechanism.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-304">**IsDebug** — karodziņš, kas norāda, vai Office būvējums ir atkļūdošanas būvējums.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-304">**IsDebug** - Flag indicating if the office build is a Debug build.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-305">Ļauj mums noteikt, vai problēmas rodas no atkļūdošanas būvējumiem, kas, iespējams, darbojas atšķirīgi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-305">Allows us to identify if issues are coming from Debug builds which may behave differently .</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-306">**IsInstalledOnExternalStorage** — karodziņš, kas norāda, vai Office ir instalēts ārējās atmiņas ierīcē.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-306">**IsInstalledOnExternalStorage** - Flag indicating if Office was installed on an external storage device.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-307">Ļauj mums noteikt, vai problēmas ir saistītas ar ārējās atmiņas ierīces atrašanās vietu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-307">Let’s us determine if issues can be traced to an external storage location.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-308">**IsOEMInstalled** — karodziņš, kas norāda, vai Office instalēja oriģinālā aprīkojuma ražotājs (OEM).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-308">**IsOEMInstalled** - Flag indicating if Office was installed by an original equipment manufacturer (OEM).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-309">Ļauj mums noteikt, vai lietojumprogramma tika instalēta, izmantojot OEM. Tas mums var palīdzēt klasificēt un noteikt problēmas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-309">Let’s us determine if the application was installed by an OEM which can help us classify and identify issues.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-310">**PreviousVersion** — Tā Office versija, kas bija iepriekš instalēta datorā.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-310">**PreviousVersion** - The version of Office that was previously installed on the machine.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-311">Ļauj atgriezties uz iepriekšējo versiju, ja pašreizējā versijā ir radusies problēma.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-311">Allows us to roll back to a previous version if the current one has an issue.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-312">**ProcessFileName** — lietojumprogrammas faila nosaukums.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-312">**ProcessFileName** - The name of the application filename.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-313">Ļauj mums noteikt tās izpildāmā procesa nosaukumu, kas ģenerē datus, jo var būt vairāki dažādu procesu failu nosaukumi, kuriem ir tās pašas programmas nosaukums.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-313">Allows us to identify the name of the executable which is generating the data as there may be several different process filenames reporting as the same app name.</span></span>

#### <a name="client"></a><span data-ttu-id="52983-314">Klients</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-314">Client</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52983-315">Informācija par Office klientu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-315">Information about the Office client.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52983-316">Šajā kategorijā ir šādi lauki:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-316">This category contains the following fields:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-317">**FirstRunTime** — pirmā reize, kad tika palaists klients.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-317">**FirstRunTime** - The first time the client was run.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-318">Ļauj izprast, cik ilgi klientā bija instalēta sistēma Office.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-318">Allows us to understand how long the client has had Office installed.</span></span>

#### <a name="device"></a><span data-ttu-id="52983-319">Ierīce</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-319">Device</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52983-320">Informācija par ierīces konfigurāciju un iespējām.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-320">Information about device configuration and capabilities.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52983-321">Šajā kategorijā ir šādi lauki:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-321">This category contains the following fields:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-322">**DigitizerInfo** — informācija par mašīnas izmantoto ciparotāju.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-322">**DigitizerInfo** - Information on the digitizer used by the machine.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-323">Ļauj mums klasificēt datus atkarībā no ierīces rakursa.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-323">Allows us to classify data based on device pivot.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-324">**FormFactor** — norāda, kādam formas faktoram atbilst ierīce, kas sūta informāciju.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-324">**FormFactor** - Identifies what form factor the device sending the info is.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-325">Ļauj mums klasificēt datus atkarībā no ierīces rakursa.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-325">Allows us to classify data based on device pivot.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-326">**FormFactorFamily** — norāda, kādam formas faktoram atbilst ierīce, kas sūta informāciju.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-326">**FormFactorFamily** - Identifies what form factor the device sending the info is.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-327">Ļauj mums klasificēt datus atkarībā no ierīces rakursa.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-327">Allows us to classify data based on device pivot.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-328">**HorizontalResolution** — horizontālā ierīces ekrāna izšķirtspēja.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-328">**HorizontalResolution** - The horizontal resolution of the devices screen.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-329">Ļauj mums klasificēt datus atkarībā no ierīces rakursa.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-329">Allows us to classify data based on device pivot.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-330">**Id** — unikāls ierīces identifikators.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-330">**Id** - A unique identifier for the device.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-331">Ļauj mums noteikt problēmu izplatību ierīču kopā.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-331">Allows us to identify the distribution of issues across a set of devices.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-332">**IsEDPPolicyEnabled** — karodziņš, kas norāda, vai mašīnā ir iespējota uzlabotā datu aizsardzība.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-332">**IsEDPPolicyEnabled** - Flag to indicate if enhanced data protection is enabled on the machine.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-333">Ļauj mums klasificēt datus atkarībā no ierīces rakursa.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-333">Allows us to classify data based on device pivot.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-334">**IsTerminalServer** — karodziņš, kas ļauj noteikt, vai mašīna ir termināļa serveris.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-334">**IsTerminalServer** - Flag to determine if the machine is a terminal server.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-335">Ļauj mums klasificēt datus atkarībā no ierīces rakursa.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-335">Allows us to classify data based on device pivot.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-336">**Manufacturer** — ierīces ražotājs.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-336">**Manufacturer** - The manufacturer of the device.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-337">Ļauj mums klasificēt datus atkarībā no ierīces rakursa.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-337">Allows us to classify data based on device pivot.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-338">**Model** — ierīces modelis.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-338">**Model** - The model of the device.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-339">Ļauj mums klasificēt datus atkarībā no ierīces rakursa.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-339">Allows us to classify data based on device pivot.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-340">**MotherboardUUIDHash** — mātesplates unikālā identifikatora jaucējkods.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-340">**MotherboardUUIDHash** - A hash of a unique identifier for the motherboard.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-341">Ļauj mums klasificēt datus atkarībā no ierīces rakursa.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-341">Allows us to classify data based on device pivot.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-342">**Name** — ierīces nosaukums.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-342">**Name** - The name of the device.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-343">Ļauj mums klasificēt datus atkarībā no ierīces rakursa.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-343">Allows us to classify data based on device pivot.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-344">**NumProcPhysCores** — fizisko kodolu skaits mašīnā.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-344">**NumProcPhysCores** - The number of physical cores on the machine.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-345">Ļauj mums klasificēt datus atkarībā no ierīces rakursa.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-345">Allows us to classify data based on device pivot.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-346">**OsLocale** — instalētās operētājsistēmas lokalizācija.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-346">**OsLocale** - The locale of the operating system that is running.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-347">Ļauj mums klasificēt datus atkarībā no ierīces rakursa.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-347">Allows us to classify data based on device pivot.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-348">**ProcessorArchitecture** — procesora arhitektūra.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-348">**ProcessorArchitecture** - The architecture of the processor.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-349">Ļauj mums klasificēt datus atkarībā no ierīces rakursa.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-349">Allows us to classify data based on device pivot.</span></span>

#### <a name="event"></a><span data-ttu-id="52983-370">Notikums</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-370">Event</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="52983-371">Notikumam raksturīga informācija, tostarp tā unikālais identifikators sesijā.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-371">Event-specific information, including its unique identifier in the session.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52983-372">Šajā kategorijā ir šādi lauki:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-372">This category contains the following fields:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-373">**Contract** — to līgumu saraksts, kurus ievieš notikums.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-373">**Contract** - A list of any contracts that the event is implementing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-374">Ļauj mums novērtēt, kādi dati ir daļa no atsevišķā notikuma, lai mēs to varētu efektīvi apstrādāt.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-374">Allows us to evaluate what data is part of the individual event so that we can process it effectively.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-375">**CV** — vērtība, kas ļauj mums noteikt savstarpēji saistītus notikumus.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-375">**CV** - A value that allows us to identify events that are related to one another.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-376">Tiek izmantota diagnostikā, ļaujot mums noteikt saistīto darbību vai notikumu modeļus.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-376">Used for diagnostics to allow us to identify patterns of related behavior or related events.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-377">**Flags** — informācija, kas tiek izmantota, lai mainītu attiecīgā notikuma atbildi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-377">**Flags** - Information used to alter how a given event responds.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-378">Tiek izmantots nolūkā pārvaldīt veidu, kā notikums tiek apstrādāts, lai augšupielādētu datus korporācijai Microsoft.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-378">Used to manage how a given event is treated for the purposes of uploading the data to Microsoft.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-379">**Id** — unikāls notikuma identifikators.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-379">**Id** - A unique identifier for the event.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-380">Ļauj mums unikāli identificēt saņemtos notikumus.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-380">Allows us to uniquely identify the events that are being received.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-381">**Name** — notikuma nosaukums.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-381">**Name** - The name of the event.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-382">Ļauj noteikt notikumu, kas tiek nosūtīts no klienta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-382">Allows to identify the event that was being sent from the client.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-383">**Rule** — tās kārtulas identifikators, kas ģenerēja datus, ja tos ģenerēja kārtula.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-383">**Rule** - An identifier of the rule that generated the data if it was generated by a rule.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-384">Ļauj mums noteikt datu avotu, lai mēs varētu pārbaudīt un pārvaldīt notikuma parametrus</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-384">Allows us to identify the source of a piece of data so that we can validate and manage that events parameters</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-385">**RuleId** — tās kārtulas identifikators, kas ģenerēja datus, ja tos ģenerēja kārtula.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-385">**RuleId** - The identifier of the rule that generated the data if it was generated by a rule.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-386">Ļauj mums noteikt datu avotu, lai mēs varētu pārbaudīt un pārvaldīt notikuma parametrus.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-386">Allows us to identify the source of a piece of data so that we can validate and manage that events parameters.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-387">**RuleInterfaces** — jebkurš interfeiss, kuru ievieš konkrēta kārtula.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-387">**RuleInterfaces** - Any interfaces that are implemented by the specific rule.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-388">Ļauj mums klasificēt un importēt datus atbilstoši to struktūrai, kas vienkāršo datu apstrādi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-388">Allows us to classify and import the data based on its structure which simplifies data processing.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-389">**RuleVersion** — tās kārtulas identifikators, kas ģenerēja datus, ja tos ģenerēja kārtula.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-389">**RuleVersion** - The identifier of the rule that generated the data if it was generated by a rule.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-390">Ļauj mums noteikt datu avotu, lai mēs varētu pārbaudīt un pārvaldīt notikuma parametrus.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-390">Allows us to identify the source of a piece of data so that we can validate and manage that events parameters.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-391">**SampleRate** — norāda, cik liels lietotāju skaits (procentos) sūta šos datus. Tas ļauj mums veikt datu statistisko analīzi un nodrošina, ka ne visiem lietotājiem ir jānosūta biežāk izmantotie datu punkti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-391">**SampleRate** - An indication of what percentage of users are sending this piece of data This allows us to do statistical analysis of the data and for very common data points not require that to be sent by all users.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-392">**SchemaVersion** — tās shēmas versija, kas tiek izmantota, lai ģenerētu diagnostikas datus.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-392">**SchemaVersion** - The version of the schema used to generate diagnostic data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-393">Nepieciešama, lai pārvaldītu datus, kas tiek sūtīti no klienta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-393">Required to manage data being sent form the client.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-394">Tādējādi laika gaitā var mainīt, kādi dati tiek sūtīti no katra klienta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-394">This allows changes over time in what data is being sent from each client.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-395">**Sequence** — skaitītājs, kas identificē secību, kādā tika ģenerēts notikums klientā.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-395">**Sequence** - A counter that identifies the order that an event was generated on the client.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-396">Ļauj kārtot saņemtos datus, lai mēs varētu noteikt darbības, kas, iespējams, izraisīja problēmu, kas ietekmē klientus.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-396">Allows the data being received to be ordered so that we can identify what steps may have led to an issue that is impacting clients.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-397">**Source** — avota kanāls, kas tika izmantots, lai augšupielādētu datus.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-397">**Source** - The source pipeline that was used to upload the data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-398">Nepieciešams, lai pārraudzītu mūsu augšupielādes kanālu vispārējo darbspēju un palīdzētu noteikt problēmas saistībā ar augšupielādes kanālu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-398">Required to monitor each of our upload pipelines for overall health and to help identify issues with the upload pipeline.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-399">Tas ļauj kontrolēt atsevišķus augšupielādes kanālus, lai nodrošinātu to atbilstību prasībām.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-399">This allows us to monitor individual upload pipelines to make sure they remain compliant.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-400">**Time** — laiks, kad klientā tika ģenerēts notikums.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-400">**Time** - The time that the event was generated on the client.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-401">Ļauj mums sinhronizēt un pārbaudīt to notikumu secību, kas ir ģenerēti klientā, kā arī izveidot veiktspējas rādītājus lietošanas norādījumiem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-401">Allows us to synchronize and validate the order of events generated on the client as well as establish performance metrics for user instructions.</span></span>

#### <a name="session"></a><span data-ttu-id="52983-419">Sesija</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-419">Session</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52983-420">Informācija par procesa sesiju.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-420">Information about the process session.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52983-421">Šajā kategorijā ir šādi lauki:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-421">This category contains the following fields:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-422">**ABConfigsDelta** — izseko atšķirībai starp pašreizējiem ABConfigs datiem un iepriekšējo vērtību.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-422">**ABConfigsDelta** - Tracks the difference between the current ABConfigs data and the previous value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-423">Ļauj mums izsekot jauniem mašīnā esošiem testējamiem variantiem, lai palīdzētu noteikt, vai problēma ir radusies jauna testējamā varianta dēļ.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-423">Allows us to track what new flights are on the machine to help identify if a new flight is responsible for an issue.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-424">**CollectibleClassification** — informācijas klases, kuras sesija var apkopot.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-424">**CollectibleClassification** - The classes of information the session can collect.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-425">Atļauj sesiju filtrēšanu, pamatojoties uz sesiju datiem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-425">Allows filtering of sessions based on the data they would have.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-426">**DisableTelemetry** — karodziņš, kas norāda, vai ir iestatīta atslēga DisableTelemetry.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-426">**DisableTelemetry** - Flag indicating if the DisableTelemetry key is set.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-427">Ļauj mums uzzināt, vai sesija ziņo par citiem diagnostikas datiem, kas nav EssentialServiceMetadata.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-427">Allows us to know if a session was not reporting diagnostic data other than EssentialServiceMetadata.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-428">**SamplingKey** — atslēga, kas tiek izmantota, lai noteiktu, vai sesija ir iztverta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-428">**SamplingKey** - The key used to determine whether the session is sampled or not.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-429">Ļauj mums saprast, kā atsevišķas sesijas izvēlas savu iztveršanas statusu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-429">Allows us to understand how individual sessions are making their choice of whether they are sampled or not.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-430">**SamplingMethod** — metode, kas tiek izmantota, lai noteiktu iztveršanas politiku.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-430">**SamplingMethod** - The method used to determine sampling policy.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-431">Ļauj mums saprast, kādi dati nāk no sesijas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-431">Allows us to understand what data is coming from a session.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-432">**Sequence** — unikāls skaitlisks sesijas identifikators.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-432">**Sequence** - A unique numeric identifier for the session.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-433">Ļauj kārtot sesijas, lai analizētu iespējamās problēmas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-433">Allows the ordering of sessions for analysis of then issues might have occurred.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-434">**Start** — procesa sesijas palaišanas laiks.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-434">**Start** - The boot time of the process session.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-435">Ļauj mums noteikt sesijas sākumu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-435">Allows us to establish when the session started.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-436">**TimeZoneBiasInMinutes** — starpība minūtēs starp UTC un vietējo laiku.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-436">**TimeZoneBiasInMinutes** - The difference in minutes between UTC and the local time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-437">Ļauj normalizēt UTC laiku atpakaļ uz vietējo laiku.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-437">Allows normalization of UTC times back to the local time.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-438">**SamplingClientIdValue** — tās atslēgas vērtība, kas tiek izmantota iztveršanas noteikšanai.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-438">**SamplingClientIdValue** - The value of the key used to determine sampling.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-439">Ļauj mums noteikt, kāpēc tika iztverta (vai neiztverta) sesija.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-439">Allows us to determine why a session was sampled or not.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-440">**SamplingDeviceIdValue** — tās atslēgas vērtība, kas tiek izmantota iztveršanas noteikšanai.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-440">**SamplingDeviceIdValue** - The value of the key used to determine sampling.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-441">Ļauj mums noteikt, kāpēc tika iztverta (vai neiztverta) sesija.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-441">Allows us to determine why a session was sampled or not.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-442">**SamplingSessionKValue** — papildu iztveršanas metadati.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-442">**SamplingSessionKValue** - Advanced sampling metadata.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-443">Izmanto, lai palīdzētu novērtēt saņemto datu statistikas nozīmi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-443">Used to help evaluate statistical meaning of data that is received.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-444">**SamplingSessionNValue** — papildu iztveršanas metadati.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-444">**SamplingSessionNValue** - Advanced sampling metadata.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-445">Izmanto, lai palīdzētu novērtēt saņemto datu statistikas nozīmi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-445">Used to help evaluate statistical meaning of data that is received.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-446">**TelemetryPermissionLevel** — vērtība, kas norāda, kāda līmeņa diagnostikas datiem ir piekritis lietotājs.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-446">**TelemetryPermissionLevel** - Value indicating what level of diagnostic data the user has opted into.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-447">Ļauj mums saprast, kāda līmeņa diagnostikas datus var sagaidīt no sesijas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-447">Allows us to understand what level of diagnostic data to expect from a session.</span></span>
