#### <a name="officecorrelationmetadatautccorrelationmetadata"></a><span data-ttu-id="52983-465">Office.CorrelationMetadata.UTCCorrelationMetadata</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-465">Office.CorrelationMetadata.UTCCorrelationMetadata</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52983-466">Nolūkā izlabot un pabeigt datus apkopo Office metadatus, izmantojot UTC, lai salīdzinātu ar līdzīgiem datiem, kas ir apkopoti, izmantojot Office telemetrijas kanālu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-466">Collects Office metadata through UTC to compare with equivalent data collected through the Office telemetry pipeline to check correctness and completeness of data.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="52983-471">**AppSessionGuid** — tās attiecīgās lietojumprogrammas sesijas identifikators, kuras sākums ir procesa izveides laiks un kas ilgst līdz procesa beigām.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-471">**AppSessionGuid** - An identifier of a particular application session starting at process creation time and persisting until process end.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-472">Tas ir formatēts kā standarta 128 bitu GUID, ko veido četras daļas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-472">It is formatted as a standard 128-bit GUID but constructed of 4 parts.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-473">Šo četru daļu secība ir: (1) 32 bitu procesa ID (2) 16 bitu sesijas ID (3) 16 bitu palaišanas ID (4) 64 bitu procesa izveides laiks: UTC 100ns</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-473">Those four parts in order are (1) 32 bit Process ID (2) 16 bit Session ID (3) 16 bit Boot ID (4) 64 bit Process creation time in UTC 100ns</span></span>

#### <a name="officetargetedmessagingensurecached"></a><span data-ttu-id="52983-492">Office.TargetedMessaging.EnsureCached</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-492">Office.TargetedMessaging.EnsureCached</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="52983-493">Izseko, vai tika lejupielādēta dinamiskās pamatnes pakotne.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-493">Tracks if a package for Dynamic Canvas was downloaded.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-494">Tiek uzskatīta par programmatūras konfigurāciju, jo pakotne ir sekmīgi jālejupielādē, lai iespējotu klientu atveidot pareizās iespējas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-494">Considered a software configuration because the package must be successfully downloaded to enable the client to render the right experience.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-495">Tas ir īpaši būtiski patērētāju abonementos, kur mēs izmantojam pamatni, lai paziņotu lietotājam par licences derīguma termiņa beigām.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-495">Is especially critical in consumer subscriptions where we use canvas to communicate to the user that the license has expired.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-496">Izmanto, lai izsekotu produkta lejupielādētās un kešotās dinamiskā satura pakotnes metadatiem, kā arī to darbību rezultātiem, kam tika pakļauta pakotne: lejupielādes kļūmēm, pakotnes atvēršanas kļūmēm, konsekvences pārbaudes kļūmēm, kešatmiņas trāpījumiem, pakotnes lietojumam un lejupielādes avotiem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-496">Used to track metadata of a dynamic content package downloaded and cached by the product as well as results of operations performed on the package: download failures, unpacking failures, consistency checks failures, cache hits, package usages, download sources.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52983-497">Tiek apkopoti tālāk norādītie lauki.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-497">The following fields are collected:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-498">**Data\_CacheFolderNotCreated —** Būla karodziņš, kas norāda, vai izdevās izveidot kešatmiņas mapi</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-498">**Data\_CacheFolderNotCreated -** Boolean flag indicating if cache folder creation succeed</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-499">**Data\_CdnPath — pakotnes avota adrese —**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-499">**Data\_CdnPath – source address of the package-**</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-500">**Data\_EnsureCached —** Būla karodziņš, kas norāda, vai tika kešota satura pakotne</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-500">**Data\_EnsureCached -** Boolean flag indicating if content package was cached</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-501">**Data\_ExistsAlready —** Būla karodziņš, kas norāda, ka pakotne jau tika iepriekš lejupielādēta un pastāv vēl viens lejupielādes mēģinājums</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-501">**Data\_ExistsAlready -** Boolean flag indicating that the package was already downloaded before and there was another attempt</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-502">**Data\_GetFileStreamFailed —** avota pakotne nav pieejama avotā</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-502">**Data\_GetFileStreamFailed -** source package not available in source</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-503">**Data\_GetFileStreamFailedToCreateLocalFolder —** lokālā diska problēmas, kas izraisa kļūmes direktorija izveides laikā</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-503">**Data\_GetFileStreamFailedToCreateLocalFolder -** local disk issues causing failure in directory creation</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-504">**Data\_GetFileStreamFromPackageFailed —** karodziņš, kas norāda, vai pakotne ir lejupielādēta, bet klients nevar to nolasīt</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-504">**Data\_GetFileStreamFromPackageFailed -** flag indicating if package was downloaded, but the client can’t read it</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-505">**Data\_GetFileStreamFromPackageSuccess —** veiksmīgi mēģinājumi lasīt pakotni</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-505">**Data\_GetFileStreamFromPackageSuccess -** successful attempts to read the package</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-506">**Data\_GetFileStreamSuccess —** nepastāv neviena ar disku vai konfigurāciju saistīta problēma, kas neatļauj lasīt failu plūsmu</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-506">**Data\_GetFileStreamSuccess -** no disk issues nor configuration issues which doesn’t let the file stream to be read</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-507">**Data\_GetRelativePathsFailed —** relatīvais ceļš nenorāda uz pieejamu atrašanās vietu</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-507">**Data\_GetRelativePathsFailed -** relative path doesn’t point to accessible location</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-508">**Data\_HashActualValue —** jaukšanas vērtība, kas tika iegūta no faila nosaukuma, lietojot pakotni</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-508">**Data\_HashActualValue -** hash value extracted from file name when the package was used</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-509">**Data\_HashCalculationFailed —** jaukšanas aprēķina kļūda</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-509">**Data\_HashCalculationFailed -** error with calculation of a hash</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-510">**Data\_HashMatchFailed —** jaukšanas neatbilstība starp pakotnes nosaukumu un kešotajām reģistra vērtībām</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-510">**Data\_HashMatchFailed -** hash mismatch between the package name and registry values cached</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-511">**Data\_HashMatchSuccess —** sekmīga jaukšanas konsekvences pārbaude</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-511">**Data\_HashMatchSuccess -** hash consistency check success</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-512">**Data\_PackageDownloadRequestFailed —** nevar lejupielādēt pakotni</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-512">**Data\_PackageDownloadRequestFailed -** can’t download the package</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-513">**Data\_PackageDownloadRequestNoData —** lejupielādētajā pakotnē nav datu</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-513">**Data\_PackageDownloadRequestNoData -** downloaded package contains no data</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-514">**Data\_PackageDownloadRequestSuccess —** sekmīgi lejupielādēta pakotne</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-514">**Data\_PackageDownloadRequestSuccess -** successful download of a package</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-515">**Data\_PackageExplodedSuccess —** pakotnes atvēršanas mēģinājumu statuss</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-515">**Data\_PackageExplodedSuccess -** unpacking attempts statuses</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-516">**Data\_PackageOpenFailed —** nesekmīgie pakotnes faila atvēršanas mēģinājumi</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-516">**Data\_PackageOpenFailed -** failed attempts to open the package file</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-517">**Data\_PackageOpenSuccess —** sekmīgie pakotnes faila atvēršanas mēģinājumi</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-517">**Data\_PackageOpenSuccess -** successful attempts to open the package file</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-518">**Data\_SuccessHashValue —** jaukšanas vērtība, kas tika iegūta no faila nosaukuma, lejupielādējot pakotni</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-518">**Data\_SuccessHashValue -** hash value extracted from file name when the package was downloaded</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-519">**Data\_SuccessSource —** virsma, kam tika lejupielādēta pakotne</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-519">**Data\_SuccessSource -** surface for which the package was downloaded</span></span>

#### <a name="officevisiovisiosku"></a><span data-ttu-id="52983-520">Office.Visio.VisioSKU</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-520">Office.Visio.VisioSKU</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52983-521">Nosaka, vai Visio SKU ir standarta vai profesionālā versija.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-521">Captures Visio SKU whether it's standard or professional.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-522">Tas ir svarīgi, lai varētu kategorizēt problēmas, kuru pamatā ir SKU.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-522">Essential to categorize issues based on SKU.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52983-523">Tiek apkopoti tālāk norādītie lauki.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-523">The following fields are collected:</span></span>

class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-548"> ExchangeGetEntitlements (and ExchangeGetManifests) could also be called on demand after host application has been running.</span></span> <span #### <a name="officefileiocsiccachedfilecsisavefilebasic"></a><span data-ttu-id="52983-933">Office.FileIO.CSI.CCachedFileCsiSaveFileBasic</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-933">Office.FileIO.CSI.CCachedFileCsiSaveFileBasic</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52983-934">Ļauj uzzināt, vai fails ir veiksmīgi saglabāts no FIO līmeņa.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-934">Allows us to know if a file was successfully saved from the FIO Layer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-935">Izmanto līdzekļu darbspējas veicināšanai un pārraudzībai.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-935">Used for Feature Health and monitoring.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52983-936">Tiek apkopoti tālāk norādītie lauki.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-936">The following fields are collected:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-937">**Activity.Group —** tags, kas ļauj grupēt pārraudzības notikumu kopu, lai pārvaldītu kopējos panākumus</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-937">**Activity.Group -** tag that allows a set of monitoring events to be grouped to manage overall success</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-938">**Activity.IsHVA —** karodziņš, kas norāda, ka šis notikums ir svarīgs lietotāja panākumiem</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-938">**Activity.IsHVA -** flag to indicate that event is critical to user success</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-939">**Data.AsyncOpen —** karodziņš, kas norāda, ka dokuments tika atvērts ar saturu, kas ir pieejams pēc galvenā satura atvēršanas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-939">**Data.AsyncOpen -** flag to indicate that the document was opened with content that arrived after the main body was opened</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-940">**Data.BaseDownloadTriggered —** izmaiņu izsekošanas diagnostika, kas norāda, ka tika pieprasīta dokumenta pamata versija</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-940">**Data.BaseDownloadTriggered -** Change tracking diagnostic indicating that the base version of the document was requested</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-941">**Data.BlockAutoUploadReasons —** iemeslu kodi bloķētajam augšupielādes statusam (piemēram, ir izslēgta automātiskā saglabāšana, dokuments ir pārejas režīmā)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-941">**Data.BlockAutoUploadReasons -** Reason codes for blocked upload state (e.g. Autosave is turned off, the document is transitioning)</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-942">**Data.BlockUploadDueToFailedSaveAsOverExisting —** augšupielāde ir bloķēta, jo mēģinot vēlreiz tā tiktu pārtraukta</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-942">**Data.BlockUploadDueToFailedSaveAsOverExisting -** Upload is blocked as it would fail if retried</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-943">**Data.CacheFileId —** izveido savienojumu ar Office dokumentu kešatmiņas telemetriju, lai iespējotu analīzi saistībā ar kešatmiņas problēmu ietekmi uz lietotāju pieredzi</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-943">**Data.CacheFileId -** connects to Office Document Cache telemetry to enable impact analysis of cache issues on the user experience</span></span>

#### <a name="officepowerpointdocoperationnewdocument"></a><span data-ttu-id="52983-1213">Office.PowerPoint.DocOperation.NewDocument</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-1213">Office.PowerPoint.DocOperation.NewDocument</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52983-1214">Apkopo, kad PowerPoint izveido jaunu prezentāciju.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-1214">Collected when PowerPoint creates a new presentation.</span></span><span data-ttu-id="52983-1215"> Ietver panākumus un veiktspējas rādītājus.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-1215"> Includes success failure and performance metrics.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52983-1216">Šī informācija tiek izmantota, lai mēs varētu sekmīgi izveidot failus, nepasliktinot veiktspēju.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-1216">This information is used to ensure we can create files successfully and with no degradation in performance.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52983-1217">Tiek apkopoti tālāk norādītie lauki.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-1217">The following fields are collected:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-1218">**NewDocumentType** — vai jaunais dokuments ir izveidots no veidnes vai vienkārši izveidots tukšs?</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-1218">**NewDocumentType** – Whether new document is created from template or just created blank?</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-1219">**FLifeguarded** — vai dokuments ir aizsargāts (līdzeklis, kas atjauno bojāta dokumenta statusu, nepaziņojot par to lietotājam)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-1219">**FLifeguarded** – Is document life guarded (feature that restores corrupt document state without prompting user)</span></span>

#### <a name="officepowerpointdocoperationopencompleteprotocol"></a><span data-ttu-id="52983-1220">Office.PowerPoint.DocOperation.OpenCompleteProtocol</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-1220">Office.PowerPoint.DocOperation.OpenCompleteProtocol</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52983-1221">Apkopo, kad PowerPoint atver prezentācijas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-1221">Collected when PowerPoint opens presentations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-1222">Tas satur informāciju, kas ir nepieciešama pareizai tādu problēmu izmeklēšanai un diagnosticēšanai, kas notiek pēdējos atvēršanas procesa posmos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-1222">It contains the information needed to be able to properly investigate and diagnose issues that happen through the end stages of the open process.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52983-1223">Microsoft izmanto šos datus, lai nodrošinātu līdzekļa pareizu darbību un neietekmētu prezentāciju atvēršanu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-1223">Microsoft uses this data to ensure the feature is working as expected and there is no degradation to opening presentations.</span></span>

#### <a name="officepowerpointdocoperationsave"></a><span data-ttu-id="52983-1279">Office.PowerPoint.DocOperation.Save</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-1279">Office.PowerPoint.DocOperation.Save</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52983-1280">Apkopots ikreiz, kad PowerPoint veic saglabāšanu, izmantojot modernu koda ceļu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-1280">Collected whenever PowerPoint performs a save using the modern code path.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-1281">Ietver saglabāšanas veiktspējas rādītāju rezultātu tipa panākumus un saistītos dokumenta metadatus.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-1281">Includes success or failure result type of save performance metrics and relevant document metadata.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-1282"> Saglabāšanas kļūmes var izraisīt datu zudumu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-1282"> Failures in save can result in data loss.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-1283">Microsoft izmanto šos datus, lai nodrošinātu, ka līdzeklis darbojas, kā paredzēts, un lietotāju saturs tiek sekmīgi turpināts.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-1283">Microsoft uses this data to ensure the feature is working as expected and user content is successfully being persisted.</span></span>

#### <a name="officepowerpointdocoperationsaveas"></a><span data-ttu-id="52983-1364">Office.PowerPoint.DocOperation.SaveAs</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-1364">Office.PowerPoint.DocOperation.SaveAs</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52983-1365">Apkopots ikreiz, kad PowerPoint veic darbību Saglabāt kā.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-1365">Collected whenever PowerPoint performs a Save As.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-1366">Ietver saglabāšanas veiktspējas rādītāju rezultātu tipa panākumus un saistītos dokumenta metadatus.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-1366">Includes success or failure result type of save performance metrics and relevant document metadata.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-1367">Saglabāšanas kļūmes var izraisīt datu zudumu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-1367">Failures in save can result in data loss.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52983-1368">Microsoft izmanto šos datus, lai nodrošinātu, ka līdzeklis darbojas, kā paredzēts, un lietotāju saturs tiek sekmīgi turpināts.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-1368">Microsoft uses this data to ensure the feature is working as expected and user content is successfully being persisted.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52983-1369">Tiek apkopoti tālāk norādītie lauki.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-1369">The following fields are collected:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-1370">**Data\_AddDocTelemetryResult:long —** vai šim žurnāla ierakstam ir visa nepieciešamā dokumenta telemetrija (Data\_Doc\_\* lauki)?</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-1370">**Data\_AddDocTelemetryResult:long -** Does this log entry have all necessary document telemetry (Data\_Doc\_\* fields)?</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-1371">Ja tā nav, kāpēc?</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-1371">If not, why?</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-1372">**Data\_CppUncaughtExceptionCount:long —** nenotverti vietējie izņēmumi darbības izpildes laikā</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-1372">**Data\_CppUncaughtExceptionCount:long -** Uncaught native exceptions while activity was running</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-1373">**Data\_DetachedDuration:long —** darbības atvienošanas/nedarbošanās ilgums</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-1373">**Data\_DetachedDuration:long -** Time for which Activity was detached/not running</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-1374">**Data\_DstDoc\_AccessMode:long —** kā šis dokuments ir atvērts (tikai lasāms | lasīšana un rakstīšana)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-1374">**Data\_DstDoc\_AccessMode:long -** How was this document opened (Read only | read write)</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-1375">**Data\_DstDoc\_AssistedReadingReasons:long —** iepriekš definētu vērtību kopa, kas norāda, kāpēc dokuments ir atvērts pieejamā lasīšanas režīmā</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-1375">**Data\_DstDoc\_AssistedReadingReasons:long -** Predefined set of values of why document was opened in assisted reading mode</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-1376">**Data\_DstDoc\_ChunkingType:long —** kā dokuments ir saglabāts pakalpojumā SharePoint</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-1376">**Data\_DstDoc\_ChunkingType:long -** How is document stored in SharePoint</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-1377">**Data\_DstDoc\_EdpState:long —** dokumenta uzņēmuma datu aizsardzība statuss</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-1377">**Data\_DstDoc\_EdpState:long -** Enterprise Data Protection state of document</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-1378">**Data\_DstDoc\_Ext:string —** dokumenta paplašinājums</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-1378">**Data\_DstDoc\_Ext:string -** Document extension</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-1379">**Data\_DstDoc\_Extension:string —** dokumenta paplašinājums</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-1379">**Data\_DstDoc\_Extension:string -** Document extension</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-1380">**Data\_DstDoc\_FileFormat:long —** iepriekš definētu faila formāta vērtību kopa (detalizētāka par paplašinājumu).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-1380">**Data\_DstDoc\_FileFormat:long -** Predefined set of values of format of file (more granular than extension)</span></span>

#### <a name="officepowerpointdocoperationsavelegacy"></a><span data-ttu-id="52983-1459">Office.PowerPoint.DocOperation.SaveLegacy</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-1459">Office.PowerPoint.DocOperation.SaveLegacy</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52983-1460">Apkopots ikreiz, kad PowerPoint veic saglabāšanu, izmantojot mantotā koda ceļu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-1460">Collected whenever PowerPoint performs a save using the legacy code path.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-1461">Ietver saglabāšanas veiktspējas rādītāju rezultātu tipa panākumus un saistītos dokumenta metadatus.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-1461">Includes success or failure result type of save performance metrics and relevant document metadata.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-1462">Saglabāšanas kļūmes var izraisīt datu zudumu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-1462">Failures in save can result in data loss.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-1463">Microsoft izmanto šos datus, lai nodrošinātu, ka līdzeklis darbojas, kā paredzēts, un lietotāju saturs tiek sekmīgi turpināts.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-1463">Microsoft uses this data to ensure the feature is working as expected and user content is successfully being persisted.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52983-1655">Izseko to lietotāju skaitam, kas saņem BizBar un dinamiskās pamatnes ziņojumus no TargetedMessagingService (TMS).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-1655">Tracks the number of users receiving BizBar and Dynamic Canvas messages from TargetedMessagingService (TMS).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-1656">Šie dati ir būtiski, jo ļauj saprast, kādus ziņojumus saņem lietotāji un kurā virsmā. <span data-ttu-id="52983-1658">Tiek apkopoti tālāk norādītie lauki.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-1658">The following fields are collected:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-1660">**Data\_Flight** — ECS/CT testējamā varianta identifikators, kas tika izmantots, lai piegādātu šo ziņojumu</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-1660">**Data\_Flight** – ECS/CT Flight identifier that was used to deliver this message</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52983-1839">Šis notikums norāda, ka lietotājs saglabā izmaiņas jaunā dokumentā.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-1839">This event indicates that a user is saving their changes to a new document.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-1840">Notikums pārrauga jauna dokumenta saglabāšanas pareizu darbību.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-1840">The event monitors whether saving to a new document is working as expected.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-1841">To izmanto arī, lai aprēķinātu mēneša aktīvos lietotājus/ierīces un mākoņpakalpojumu uzticamības rādītājus.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-1841">It is also used to calculated monthly active users/devices and cloud reliability metrics.</span></span>

#### <a name="officewordfilesaveactfconfirmsavedoccoreautorecoverysave"></a><span data-ttu-id="52983-1887">Office.Word.FileSave.ActFConfirmSaveDocCoreAutoRecoverySave</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-1887">Office.Word.FileSave.ActFConfirmSaveDocCoreAutoRecoverySave</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52983-1888">Šis notikums norāda, ka Office Word saglabā automātiski atkoptu dokumentu, kas nav bijis saglabāts iepriekš.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-1888">This event indicates Office Word saves an auto-recovery document that has not been saved before.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-1889">Tādējādi Microsoft var noteikt automātiskās atkopšanas kļūdas, kam ir būtiska nozīme dokumenta datu aizsardzībā.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-1889">It allows Microsoft to detect errors in auto-recovery which is important for document data safety.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52983-1890">Notikums pārrauga automātiski atkopta dokumenta saglabāšanas pareizu darbību.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-1890">The event monitors whether auto-recovery-save is working as expected.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-1891">To izmanto arī, lai aprēķinātu mēneša aktīvos lietotājus/ierīces un mākoņpakalpojumu uzticamības rādītājus.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-1891">It is also used to calculated monthly active users/devices and cloud reliability metrics.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52983-1892">Tiek apkopoti tālāk norādītie lauki.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-1892">The following fields are collected:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-1894">**Data\_Doc\_AccessMode —** dokuments ir tikai lasāms/rediģējams</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-1894">**Data\_Doc\_AccessMode -** Document is read only/editable</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-1897">**Data\_Doc\_EdpState —** dokumenta elektronisko datu aizsardzības iestatījums</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-1897">**Data\_Doc\_EdpState -** Electronic Data Protection setting for the document</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-1898">**Data\_Doc\_Ext —** dokumentu paplašinājums (docx/xlsb/pptx utt.)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-1898">**Data\_Doc\_Ext -** Document extension (docx/xlsb/pptx etc.)</span></span>

#### <a name="officewordfilesaveactfconfirmsavedoccorequerysave"></a><span data-ttu-id="52983-1937">Office.Word.FileSave.ActFConfirmSaveDocCoreQuerySave</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-1937">Office.Word.FileSave.ActFConfirmSaveDocCoreQuerySave</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52983-1938">Šis notikums norāda, ka Office Word aicina lietotāju saglabāt izmaiņas, kad tiek mēģināts aizvērt dokumentu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-1938">This event indicates Office Word prompts the user to save changes when it tries to close the document.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-1939">Tas ļauj korporācijai Microsoft pārraudzīt, vai saglabāšana pēc programmas aizvēršanas darbojas pareizi un netiek zaudēti dati.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-1939">It allows Microsoft to monitor whether save-at-quit works as expected to avoid document data loss.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-1940">Notikums pārrauga, vai dokumenta saglabāšana pēc programmas aizvēršanas darbojas pareizi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-1940">The event monitors whether save-at-quit is working as expected.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-1941">To izmanto arī, lai aprēķinātu mēneša aktīvos lietotājus/ierīces un mākoņpakalpojumu uzticamības rādītājus.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-1941">It is also used to calculated monthly active users/devices and cloud reliability metrics.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52983-1942">Tiek apkopoti tālāk norādītie lauki.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-1942">The following fields are collected:</span></span>

#### <a name="officewordfilesavesaveassavefile"></a><span data-ttu-id="52983-1998">Office.Word.FileSave.SaveAsSaveFile</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-1998">Office.Word.FileSave.SaveAsSaveFile</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52983-1999">Šis notikums norāda, ka Office Word saglabā dokumentu jaunā dokumentā.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-1999">This event indicates Office Word saves a document into a new document.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-2000">Tādējādi Microsoft var noteikt darbības “saglabāt kā” kļūdas, kam ir būtiska nozīme, lai novērstu dokumenta datu zudumu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2000">It allows Microsoft to detect errors in save-as which is important to avoid document data loss.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-2001">Notikums pārrauga, vai dokumenta saglabāšana darbojas pareizi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2001">The event monitors whether save-as is working as expected.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-2002">To izmanto arī, lai aprēķinātu mēneša aktīvos lietotājus/ierīces un mākoņpakalpojumu uzticamības rādītājus.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2002">It is also used to calculated monthly active users/devices and cloud reliability metrics.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-2006">**Data\_AddDocTelemResDst —** norāda, vai mēs varam pareizi aizpildīt citas ar dokumentu telemetriju saistītās vērtības šajā notikumā mērķa dokumentam.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2006">**Data\_AddDocTelemResDst -** Reports whether we were able to properly populate other document telemetry related values in the event for the destination document.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-2007">Izmanto datu kvalitātes diagnostikai.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2007">Used for data quality diagnostics.</span></span>

#### <a name="officewordworddocumentdirtyflagchanged"></a><span data-ttu-id="52983-2120">Office.Word.Word.DocumentDirtyFlagChanged</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2120">Office.Word.Word.DocumentDirtyFlagChanged</span></span>

#### <a name="officevisiosharedfeatureexperimentation"></a><span data-ttu-id="52983-2136">Office.Visio.Shared.FeatureExperimentation</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2136">Office.Visio.Shared.FeatureExperimentation</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52983-2137">Reģistrē līdzekļu izmēģinājumus lietotājiem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2137">Tracks feature flighting for users.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-2138">Šis notikums palīdz mums noteikt līdzekļa izmēģinājuma izdošanos vai neveiksmi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2138">This event helps us determines success or failure of feature flights.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52983-2139">Tiek apkopoti tālāk norādītie lauki.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2139">The following fields are collected:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="52983-2588">**AppSessionGuid** — tās attiecīgās lietojumprogrammas sesijas identifikators, kuras sākums ir procesa izveides laiks un kas ilgst līdz procesa beigām.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2588">**AppSessionGuid** - An identifier of a particular application session starting at process creation time and persisting until process end.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-2589">Tas ir formatēts kā standarta 128 bitu GUID, ko veido četras daļas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2589">It is formatted as a standard 128-bit GUID but constructed of 4 parts.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-2590">Šo četru daļu secība ir: (1) 32 bitu procesa ID (2) 16 bitu sesijas ID (3) 16 bitu palaišanas ID (4) 64 bitu procesa izveides laiks: UTC 100ns</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2590">Those four parts in order are (1) 32 bit Process ID (2) 16 bit Session ID (3) 16 bit Boot ID (4) 64 bit Process creation time in UTC 100ns</span></span>

#### <a name="officetelemetryenginesessionhandoff"></a><span data-ttu-id="52983-2604">Office.TelemetryEngine.SessionHandOff</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2604">Office.TelemetryEngine.SessionHandOff</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="52983-2611">**appVersionMinor** — programmas papildversijas numurs.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2611">**appVersionMinor** - The app minor version number.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="52983-2612">**appVersionRev** — programmas pārskatītās versijas numurs.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2612">**appVersionRev** - The app revision version number.</span></span>

#### <a name="officewordfileopenopencmdfilemrupriv"></a><span data-ttu-id="52983-2615">Office.Word.FileOpen.OpenCmdFileMruPriv</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2615">Office.Word.FileOpen.OpenCmdFileMruPriv</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52983-2616">Šis notikums norāda, ka Office Word atver dokumentu no pēdējo lietoto dokumentu saraksta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2616">This event indicates Office Word opens a document from the Most Recent Used (MRU) list.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-2617">Tas satur arī kritiski svarīgus faila atvēršanas izpildes datus, un no lietotāja skatpunkta ir programmas startēšanas notikums.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2617">It also contains critical file open performance data, and is an app start event from user perspective.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-2618">Notikums pārrauga, vai faila atvēršana no pēdējo lietoto dokumentu saraksta darbojas pareizi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2618">The event monitors whether file-open-from-MRU is working as expected.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-2619">To izmanto arī, lai aprēķinātu mēneša aktīvos lietotājus/ierīces un mākoņpakalpojumu uzticamības rādītājus.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2619">It is also used to calculated monthly active users/devices, and cloud reliability metrics.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-2623">**Data\_BytesAsynchronous —** baitu skaits (saspiests), bez kura uzskatām, ka varēsim atvērt failu, ja tos iegūstam pirms lietotājs vēlas sākt rediģēšanu vai saglabāšanu</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2623">**Data\_BytesAsynchronous -** Number of bytes (compressed) that we believe we can open the file without if we get them before the user wants to start editing or maybe saving</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-2625">**Data\_BytesSynchronous —** baitu skaits (saspiests), kuram jābūt mūsu rīcībā, pirms varam sākt faila atvēršanu</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2625">**Data\_BytesSynchronous -** Number of bytes (compressed) that we must have before we can start opening the file</span></span>

#### <a name="officewordfileopenopenffileopenxstzcore"></a><span data-ttu-id="52983-2681">Office.Word.FileOpen.OpenFFileOpenXstzCore</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2681">Office.Word.FileOpen.OpenFFileOpenXstzCore</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52983-2682">Šis notikums norāda, ka Office Word atver dokumentu, uz kura lietotājs veic dubultklikšķi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2682">This event indicates Office Word opens a document who is double clicked by a user.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-2683">Tas satur arī kritiski svarīgus faila atvēršanas izpildes datus, un no lietotāja skatpunkta ir programmas startēšanas notikums.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2683">It also contains critical file open performance data, and is an app start event from user perspective.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-2684">Notikums pārrauga, vai faila atvēršana ar dubultklikšķi darbojas pareizi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2684">The event monitors whether file-open-from-file-double-click is working as expected.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-2685">To izmanto arī, lai aprēķinātu mēneša aktīvos lietotājus/ierīces un mākoņpakalpojumu uzticamības rādītājus.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2685">It is also used to calculated monthly active users/devices, and cloud reliability metrics.</span></span>

#### <a name="officewordfileopenopenifrinitargs"></a><span data-ttu-id="52983-2747">Office.Word.FileOpen.OpenIfrInitArgs</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2747">Office.Word.FileOpen.OpenIfrInitArgs</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52983-2748">Šis notikums norāda, ka Office Word atver dokumentu, izmantojot COM aktivizēšanu vai komandrindu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2748">This event indicates Office Word opens a document via COM activation or command line.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-2749">Tas satur arī kritiski svarīgus faila atvēršanas izpildes datus, un no lietotāja skatpunkta ir programmas startēšanas notikums.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2749">It also contains critical file open performance data, and is an app start event from user perspective.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-2750">Notikums pārrauga, vai faila atvēršana no komandrindas darbojas pareizi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2750">The event monitors whether file-open-from-command-line is working as expected.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-2751">To izmanto arī, lai aprēķinātu mēneša aktīvos lietotājus/ierīces un mākoņpakalpojumu uzticamības rādītājus.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2751">It is also used to calculated monthly active users/devices, and cloud reliability metrics.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52983-2752">Tiek apkopoti tālāk norādītie lauki.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2752">The following fields are collected:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-2753">**Data\_AddDocTelemRes —** norāda, vai mēs varam pareizi aizpildīt citas ar dokumentu telemetriju saistītās vērtības šajā notikumā.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2753">**Data\_AddDocTelemRes -** Reports whether we were able to properly populate other document telemetry related values in the event.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-2754">Izmanto datu kvalitātes diagnostikai.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2754">Used for data quality diagnostics.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-2755">**Data\_BytesAsynchronous —** baitu skaits (saspiests), bez kura uzskatām, ka varēsim atvērt failu, ja tos iegūstam pirms lietotājs vēlas sākt rediģēšanu vai saglabāšanu</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2755">**Data\_BytesAsynchronous -** Number of bytes (compressed) that we believe we can open the file without if we get them before the user wants to start editing or maybe saving.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-2756">**Data\_BytesAsynchronousWithWork —** baitu skaits (saspiests), bez kura, iespējams, varēsim atvērt failu, taču tam būs nepieciešamas būtiskas koda izmaiņas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2756">**Data\_BytesAsynchronousWithWork -** Number of bytes (compressed) that we might be able to open the file without but would require significant code investments to make it happen</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-2757">**Data\_BytesSynchronous —** baitu skaits (saspiests), kuram jābūt mūsu rīcībā, pirms varam sākt faila atvēršanu</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2757">**Data\_BytesSynchronous -** Number of bytes (compressed) that we must have before we can start opening the file</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-2758">**Data\_BytesUnknown —** baitu skaits dokumenta daļās, kuras neplānojam atrast</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2758">**Data\_BytesUnknown -** Number of bytes in document parts that we don’t expect to find.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-2759">**Data\_Doc\_AccessMode —** dokuments ir tikai lasāms/rediģējams</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2759">**Data\_Doc\_AccessMode -** Document is read only/editable</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-2760">**Data\_Doc\_AssistedReadingReasons —** iepriekš definētu vērtību kopa, kas norāda, kāpēc dokuments ir atvērts pieejamā lasīšanas režīmā</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2760">**Data\_Doc\_AssistedReadingReasons -** Predefined set of values of why document was opened in assisted reading mode</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-2761">**Data\_Doc\_ChunkingType —** vienības, kas tiek izmantotas inkrementālā dokumenta atvēršanā</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2761">**Data\_Doc\_ChunkingType -** Units used for incremental document open</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-2762">**Data\_Doc\_EdpState —** dokumenta elektronisko datu aizsardzības iestatījums</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2762">**Data\_Doc\_EdpState -** Electronic Data Protection setting for the document</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-2763">**Data\_Doc\_Ext —** dokumentu paplašinājums (docx/xlsb/pptx utt.)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2763">**Data\_Doc\_Ext -** Document extension (docx/xlsb/pptx, etc.)</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-2764">**Data\_Doc\_FileFormat —** faila formāta protokola versija</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2764">**Data\_Doc\_FileFormat -** File format protocol version</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-2765">**Data\_Doc\_Fqdn —** OneDrive vai SharePoint Online domēna nosaukums</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2765">**Data\_Doc\_Fqdn -** OneDrive or SharePoint Online Domain Name</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-2766">**Data\_Doc\_FqdnHash —** klientu identificējama domēna nosaukuma vienvirziena jaukšana</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2766">**Data\_Doc\_FqdnHash -** One-way hash of customer identifiable domain name</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-2767">**Data\_Doc\_IOFlags —** atskaites par kešotajiem karodziņiem, kas tiek izmantoti pieprasījuma opciju iestatīšanai</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2767">**Data\_Doc\_IOFlags -** Reports on the cached flags used to set open request options</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-2768">**Data\_Doc\_IdentityTelemetryId —** tādas lietotāja identitātes vienvirziena jaukšana, kas tiek izmantota atvēršanā</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2768">**Data\_Doc\_IdentityTelemetryId -** A one-way hash of the user identity used to perform the open</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-2769">**Data\_Doc\_InitializationScenario —** dokumenta atvēršanas ieraksti</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2769">**Data\_Doc\_InitializationScenario -** Records how the document was opened</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-2770">**Data\_Doc\_IrmRights —** dokumentam/lietotājam piemērotās elektronisko datu politikas atļautās darbības</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2770">**Data\_Doc\_IrmRights -** Actions permitted by the Electronic Data Protection policy that has been applied to the document/user</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-2771">**Data\_Doc\_IsIncrementalOpen —** karodziņš, kas norāda, ka dokuments ir atvērts inkrementāli</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2771">**Data\_Doc\_IsIncrementalOpen -** Flag indicating that the document has been incrementally opened</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-2772">**Data\_Doc\_IsOcsSupported —** karodziņš, kas norāda, ka dokuments tiek atbalstīts sadarbības pakalpojumā</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2772">**Data\_Doc\_IsOcsSupported -** Flag indicating that the document is supported in the collaboration service</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-2773">**Data\_Doc\_IsOpeningOfflineCopy —** atzīme, kas norāda, ka tika atvērta dokumenta bezsaistes kopija</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2773">**Data\_Doc\_IsOpeningOfflineCopy -** Flag indicating that the offline copy of a document was opened</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-2780">**Data\_Doc\_ReadOnlyReasons —** iemesli, kāpēc dokuments ir atvērts tikai lasāmajā režīmā</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2780">**Data\_Doc\_ReadOnlyReasons -** Reasons why the document was opened read only</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-2787">**Data\_Doc\_SharePointServiceContext —** diagnostikas informācija no SharePoint Online pieprasījumiem</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2787">**Data\_Doc\_SharePointServiceContext -** Diagnostic information from SharePoint Online requests</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-2791">**Data\_Doc\_SyncBackedType —** norāda dokumenta veidu (lokālais vai servera)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2791">**Data\_Doc\_SyncBackedType -** Indicator as to the type of document (local or service based)</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-2794">**Data\_EditorDisablingRename —** tā pirmā redaktora identifikators, kas izraisīja pārdēvēšanas atspējošanu</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2794">**Data\_EditorDisablingRename -** Identifier of the first editor that caused for rename to be disabled</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-2795">**Data\_EditorsCount —** redaktoru skaits dokumentā</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2795">**Data\_EditorsCount -** Number of editors in the document</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-2796">**Datu\_FSucceededAfterRecoverableFailure —** norāda, ka atvēršana izdevās pēc kļūmes izlabošanas, kas radās dokumenta atvēršanas laikā</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2796">**Data\_FSucceededAfterRecoverableFailure -** Indicates that open succeeded after repairing a failure while opening the document</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-2800">**Data\_MainPdod —** dokumenta identifikators Office Word procesā</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2800">**Data\_MainPdod -** The document identifier in Office Word process</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-2803">**Data\_MoveDisabledReason —** kļūda, kas atspējo dokumenta pārvietošanu</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2803">**Data\_MoveDisabledReason -** Error that is disabling move for the document</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-2804">**Data\_MoveFlightEnabled —** vai lidojuma opcija pārvietošanas līdzeklī ir iespējota</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2804">**Data\_MoveFlightEnabled -** Whether the flight for the move feature is enabled</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-2805">**Data\_PartsUnknown —** dokumenta daļu skaits, kurām mēs nevarējām iegūt datus</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2805">**Data\_PartsUnknown -** the number of document parts that we couldn’t get data for</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-2811">**Data\_UsesNormal —** norāda, vai atvērtā dokumenta pamatā ir parasta veidne</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2811">**Data\_UsesNormal -** Indicates whether the open document is based on the normal template.</span></span>


#### <a name="officewordfileopenopenloadfile"></a><span data-ttu-id="52983-2812">Office.Word.FileOpen.OpenLoadFile</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2812">Office.Word.FileOpen.OpenLoadFile</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52983-2813">Šis notikums norāda, ka Office Word atver dokumentu, izmantojot atvēršanas dialoglodziņu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2813">This event indicates Office Word opens a document via Open dialog.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-2814">Tas satur arī kritiski svarīgus faila atvēršanas izpildes datus, un no lietotāja skatpunkta ir programmas startēšanas notikums.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2814">It also contains critical file open performance data, and is an app start event from user perspective.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-2815">Notikums pārrauga, vai faila atvēršana no atvēršanas dialoglodziņa darbojas pareizi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2815">The event monitors whether file-open-from-the-open-file-dialog is working as expected.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-2816">To izmanto arī, lai aprēķinātu mēneša aktīvos lietotājus/ierīces un mākoņpakalpojumu uzticamības rādītājus.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2816">It is also used to calculated monthly active users/devices, and cloud reliability metrics.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52983-2817">Tiek apkopoti tālāk norādītie lauki.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2817">The following fields are collected:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-2818">**Data\_AddDocTelemRes —** norāda, vai mēs varam pareizi aizpildīt citas ar dokumentu telemetriju saistītās vērtības šajā notikumā.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2818">**Data\_AddDocTelemRes -** Reports whether we were able to properly populate other document telemetry related values in the event.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-2819">Izmanto datu kvalitātes diagnostikai.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2819">Used for data quality diagnostics.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-2820">**Data\_BytesAsynchronous —** baitu skaits (saspiests), bez kura uzskatām, ka varēsim atvērt failu, ja tos iegūstam pirms lietotājs vēlas sākt rediģēšanu vai saglabāšanu</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2820">**Data\_BytesAsynchronous -** Number of bytes (compressed) that we believe we can open the file without if we get them before the user wants to start editing or maybe saving</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-2821">**Data\_BytesAsynchronousWithWork —** baitu skaits (saspiests), bez kura, iespējams, varēsim atvērt failu, taču tam būs nepieciešamas būtiskas koda izmaiņas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2821">**Data\_BytesAsynchronousWithWork -** Number of bytes (compressed) that we might be able to open the file without but would require significant code investments to make it happen</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-2822">**Data\_BytesSynchronous —** baitu skaits (saspiests), kuram jābūt mūsu rīcībā, pirms varam sākt faila atvēršanu</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2822">**Data\_BytesSynchronous -** Number of bytes (compressed) that we must have before we can start opening the file</span></span>

#### <a name="officeaccessibilityaccessibilitytoolsessionpresencewin32"></a><span data-ttu-id="52983-2879">Office.Accessibility.AccessibilityToolSessionPresenceWin32</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2879">Office.Accessibility.AccessibilityToolSessionPresenceWin32</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52983-2880">Ļauj mums noteikt, vai lietotājam ir palīgtehnoloģiju rīks, un tā nosaukumu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2880">Allows us to detect that the user has an Assistive technology tool and its name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-2881">Tas ļauj saprast, vai Office lietotājam ir radušās problēmas ar konkrētu palīgtehnoloģiju rīku.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2881">This allows us to understand if an Office user is experiencing issues with a specific Assistive Technology tool.</span></span>

#### <a name="officewordaccessibilitylearningtoolsreadaloudplayreadaloud"></a><span data-ttu-id="52983-2892">Office.Word.Accessibility.LearningTools.ReadAloud.PlayReadAloud</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2892">Office.Word.Accessibility.LearningTools.ReadAloud.PlayReadAloud</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52983-2893">Šis notikums norāda, vai Office Word lasa dokumenta tekstu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2893">This event indicates Office Word reads aloud the text in the document.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-2894">Šis notikums ir pieejamības līdzekļa periodiskais kontrolziņojums, kas ļauj Microsoft izvērtēt teksta lasīšanas līdzekļa darbspēju.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2894">The event is a heartbeat of the accessibility feature which allows Microsoft to evaluate the feature health of read-aloud-text.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52983-2895">Tiek apkopoti tālāk norādītie lauki.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2895">The following fields are collected:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="52983-2897">**Data\_CharactersWithSpaceCount —** dokumenta rakstzīmju un atstarpju skaits</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-2897">**Data\_CharactersWithSpaceCount -** character and space count of the document</span></span>

#### <a name="officemanageabilityserviceapplypolicy"></a><span data-ttu-id="52983-3073">Office.Manageability.Service.ApplyPolicy</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-3073">Office.Manageability.Service.ApplyPolicy</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52983-3074">Kritiski svarīgi telemetrijas dati, lai izsekotu kļūmi\\Sekmīgi lietoti mākoņa politikas iestatījumi reģistrā.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-3074">Critical telemetry to track failure\\Success of applying cloud policy settings to registry.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52983-3075">LastError norāda, kāpēc un kur neizdevās politikas lietošana reģistrā.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52983-3075">LastError tells why and where the Application of policy in registry failed.</span></span>
